              <span class="facet--color-swatch tag--color-swatch" data-bind="css: getColorClass(getLabel())"></span>
              <span class="tag--color-text" data-bind="html: getValue()"></span>
            </span>
          <!-- /ko -->
          <!-- ko if: isStyle() -->
            <span class="tag--text" data-bind="html: getValue()"></span>
          <!-- /ko -->
          <!-- ko if: !isColor() && !isStyle() -->
            <span class="tag--text" data-bind="html: getLabel()"></span>
          <!-- /ko -->
      </span>
    </button>
  <!-- /ko -->
</script>
